no boss battle at this time, just a lot of scenes.

SITUATION BONUS [Reached Svala within 3 minutes.] yields MALUS WOOD, in case
you were fast enough. This also bags achievement <IMPERIAL GUARD> on your tab.
Now sit back and enjoy some scenes.

-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-
CHAPTER #035 - DREAM OF THE PAST
-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-

Sit back, grab some chips and enjoy the scenes.

-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-
CHAPTER #036 - PROMISES
-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-

Your next destination is set - a place called Dais, NW in Cobasna. Come on, I'm
bored to death with that forest... but Mandragoras are hawt.

Touma joins as lv28 chr, and comes equipped with WEATHER FOX, CRESTED VEST,
CRESTED MASK, BALSA CLOGS. Komachi joins as lv28 chr, and comes equipped with
SPARROW, CRESTED VEST, CRESTED MASK, BALSA CLOGS.

Komachi is second chr that can open locked chests, and disable traps on trapped
chests. Additionally, when you Komachi Connect, she has a skill Honeybiteme...
er, I mean, Honeysuckme... what in the world is wrong with me? *gets ass kicked
by Aya* Focus! OK, she has a skill called Honeysuckle which can get you the
contents of those distant chests you've been seeing.

There's new equips available as well, and you can find Faina and Leif near the
entrance to chapel on first floor. I suggest to buy lots of paralysis removal
items.

Dominica Connect and talk to Vic to unlock Dominica's Trait 3, and change Vic's
Trait 3.

Talk to Edward in the library to change Edward's Trait 3.

Rucha Connect and talk to Rico for funny scene.

Aya Connect and talk to Gustav to change Aya's Trait 3 and Gustav's Trait 4.

Michelle Connect and talk to Komachi to unlock Michelle's Trait 2.

Savio Connect and talk to Kiriya to unlock Kiriya's Trait 2.

Eugene Connect and talk to Touma for a scene.

QUEST 30 START & COMPLETION - CASANDRA RING
Eugene Connect and talk to aristo Karin (3rd floor, NW end). Svala lost
something important to her and wants you to find it. One of imperial guards in
front of her room will have a theory on an animal sneaking off with the ring.
Rico Connect and talk to the mouse David in one of the rooms (2nd floor, W
side) to obtain CRESTED RING KI. Eugene Connect and talk to Karin again, then
talk to Svala to receive CASANDRA RING.

QUEST 31 START - REPLICA KATANA
Komachi Connect and talk to Shido (2nd floor, E side) - he has misplaced some
katana given to him by Shinkai. Let's do exactly what he fears - talk to
Shinkai in the library on 2nd floor. You'll need Lizard Fang (dropped by drogos
in Cobasna), Rachnuvus Cloth (dropped by spiders in Dais), and Titanium Metal
(buy from Faina in Halgita).

QUEST 32 START & COMPLETION - VIC'S FASHION SENSE
Vic Connect and talk to Lavie (2nd floor, E side) - she wants you to bring her
Barkcloth and 3x Golden Wolf Fur. If you have these items in your inventory,
talk to her again to give them away. Return after 30 gameplay minutes to obtain
GOLDEN FUR JACKET.

QUEST 33 START & COMPLETION - HELPING OUT THE SHOPS
Talk to Owen in the chapel on 1st floor. Halgita's shops are in need of help.
Word of advice - after you help out a shop, shop's warez will change, so make
sure you buy 99 of all materials they have available!
- Talk to 'Lively shopkeeper' on 1st floor, and bring her 3x Lentesco Wood (you
  can buy some from Faina). Once you do, you get BLUE BERRY POWDER,
  WHITE BERRY POWDER and shop's warez change.
- Talk to 'Hardworking weaponsmith' on B1 floor and give him 150000 fol. You'll
  get SYMPHONIC BATON and shop's warez change.
- Talk to 'Quiet armor shopkeeper' - trade route to Kolton has been blocked by
  some lizardmen. Leave Halgita and schlepp yourself back to Kolton. In the
  tunnel before the teleporter you'll see that some drogo warriors have spawned
  (around 10 total). Kill them all, then report back to get GARUDA HOOD and
  shop's warez change.
- Finally talk to Owen to obtain FLYING SWALLOW.

You can do second dog quest in Kolton now.

===============================================================================
KOLTON
===============================================================================

QUEST 34 START & COMPLETION - DOG WOES, SECOND STRIKE
Rico Connect and talk to 'Aspiring animal breeder' in front of the bar. Her dog
ran away again, and she wants to know why. Find the dog in E part of the city
and talk to it. Okay, exercise, I get it. Return to 'Aspiring animal breeder',
talk to her. Done! Return after 30 minutes... and you get MERCURIUS WRISTGUARD.

Return to Halgita and do some Horseshoes crafting to regain fol you spent.
Faina is closer to the entrance here than the first shop in Kolton.

When rolling in fol, leave for Cobasna. Your party should include Komachi and
Rico.

===============================================================================
COBASNA TIMBERLANDS
===============================================================================

Dais is in NW corner of Cobasna. Difficult to find, perhaps, but you have some
help - whenever you reach a cross, look at the paths leading in different
directions. Above one of them you will see green lights emanating from the
ground, denoting correct direction to the Dais!

If green lights are mixed with purple, there's nothing wrong with that, purple
lights merely denote right direction to Kiriya's house we've visited earlier.

So from entering Cobasna, go N, W at the cross, N at the cross, N at the cross,
N at the cross, W at the cross, open BSCH for MEMOIRS OF AN ALCHEMIST, N at the
cross, step into the warp, N, E at the cross, step into the warp, there's WCH
with LIZARD SKIN VEST behind you, continue N and you're in Dais.

-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-
CHAPTER #037 - NATURE'S MAZE
-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-

===============================================================================
DAIS
===============================================================================

As soon as you're in, you're attacked by a bunch of spiders. Defeat them all,
then save at SPN - there is only one more SPN at the top, and you have to get
thru a boss to reach it, so be careful.

1ST FLOOR

Take N path to a cross, and then go NW - Komachi Connect and use Ash on the web
to remove it, then kill some small spiders that will appear. At the dead end is
locked SCH with HALGITIAN PAPER. Return to cross and take NE path to reach a
room with two further paths - E one is dead end with a scorpion, and S one will
eventually put you in SPN room. Before that there is small dead end with two
chests - MCH will turn into Iron Chest Mimic, WCH has RED BERRY POWDER in it.

Back in SPN room, take S path, Aya Connect and use Cardinal Cloak on the web,
then take path branching S to dead end with a spider, and then return to cross
and waltz W. Don't touch the shrooms as they will confuse you, and it's not
pretty watching Aya tearing Capell apart (more action for me, though).

When you approach the pit, a spider will be shown how to cross it. Press on.

2ND FLOOR

Squish everything, go E at 1stcross, kill two Iron Chest Mimics (silly MCH),
back to 1stcross, go S, wait for spidey-bridge, press on.

3RD FLOOR

Aya Connect and Cardinal Cloak the web, then go E, and play Percipere near
familiar sound source to uncover BSCH with RACHNUVUS CLOTH. Back and continue
SW - wait for spidey-bridge, press on, wait for next spidey-bridge. You've come
to 1stcross, go NW, Aya Connect and Cardinal Cloak on the web, smash all
enemies, open WCH for PARA-GONE. Back to 1stcross, E, wait for spidey-bridge,
2ndcross, go N for dead end with a spider, back to 2ndcross, go S to reach
3rdcross, go E for dead end with locked SCH with ANTIDOTE. DO NOT OPEN BSCH
WITH CAPELL! It contains petrify trap and if everyone is affected, Game Over!
Komachi Connect and open BSCH with GENIUS'S QUILL (gas trap). Back to 3rdcross,
SW, wait for spidey-bridge, then press on.

4TH FLOOR

Aya Connect and Cardinal Cloak the web, continue to 1stcross, go E to dead end
with three scorpions, back to 1stcross, go W and press on.

5TH FLOOR

There's a clearing with three exits, and a spider is parked on the E side. Make
spidey-bridge to E, then make the spider follow you to either W or N exit. What
you need to do is go left/right in front of the pit and wait for spider to
shoot the webbing, hopefully missing you and creating spidey-bridge at the same
time. This is a super-easy process if you brought Rico along - I didn't, so I
had to do it the hard way.

W exit takes you to a fork in the path - one leads to a dead end with MCH (Iron
Box Mimic), and the other to a room full of spiders (also need to Aya Connect
and Cardinal Cloak the web).

N exit takes you to another dead end. Look around and you'll spot BSCH on the
wall - Komachi Connect and Honeysuckle BSCH for RACHNUVUS PUMPS.

Take E exit now - continue to 1stcross, NW for dead end with three chests - one
is MCH that turns into Iron Chest Mimic, trapped WCH has WHITE BERRY POTION
(gas trap), and locked SCH has MALUS WOOD. Back to 1stcross, SE, Aya Connect
and Cardinal Cloak the web, press on.

6TH FLOOR

At 1stcross go W, and play Percipere near familiar sound to uncover BSCH with
PRISMATITE SWORD. Back to 1stcross and stop... N path leads to boss battle. As
I said before, there's no save before it, so if you feel the need to be safe,
travel all the way down to 1st floor to save. When you return, continue the
climb until a scene pops up.

------------------------ HERE COMES A NEW CHALLENGER! -------------------------
Main Combatant/s: QUEEN RACHNUVUS [76850 HP]          EXP: 6300    FOL: 3000
        ELEM-RES: Air: 100, Fire: 250, Earth: 100, Aether:  50, Water: 250
          SKILLS: Poisonous Venom
                  [Reinforcements spawn]
                  [Ramming attack]
Side Combatant/s: CAVE RACHNUVUSes, LARVAe, SCISSORCLAW CENTIPEDEs
Environmental hazard: none
------------------------------ GET READY! FIGHT! ----------------- Capell lv038
Queen will be blocking the exit, and every so often use a move against you.
First obliterate everything that crawls and doesn't resemble the queen. Once
you've stimped all the little guys, boss comes out and you can damage it
without fear of counters. While boss is out, it'll summon more reinforcements,
then retreat again.

Don't stand too close to the queen when it's blocking the exit, or fear
needless damage. Each time when new spideys enter the battle, squish them, wait
for queen to come out and damage it. Capell's Reginleif deals tremendous damage
in thousands, and can very well save the day.

Also make sure you're stocked up on Para-Gones to cure paralysis, otherwise it
can spell the death of your team.
-------------------- CONGRATULATIONS! YOU ARE AYATORIOUS! ---------------------

If you succeed in dropping stalactites on the queen, thus killing her, you win
SITUATION BONUS [Used stalactite to finish the rachnuvus queen.] for some
RACHNUVUS CLOTH.

Continue N, open BSCH for ODIOUS EYE, WCH for PANACEA, and you're at the top.
Open two BSCH for OVERTURE NOTATIONS KI, SILK ROBE. Make sure to save at SPN
before going on!

------------------------ HERE COMES A NEW CHALLENGER! -------------------------
Main Combatant/s: HELD [60000 HP]                     EXP: ????    FOL: ????
        ELEM-RES: Air:  50, Fire: 100, Earth: 100, Aether: 250, Water: 100
          SKILLS: Undyn
                  Spin Axis
Side Combatant/s: FAESPHEREs [4000 HP]
Environmental hazard: none
------------------------------ GET READY! FIGHT! ----------------- Capell lv039
Kiriya and Savio join the battle as NPCs with infinite HP. Still, if everyone
on your team dies, it's Game Over, as Kiriya and Savio can't revive you.

Faespheres will keep popping up during the battle, so try to destroy them to
limit the damage Held can do to you. Otherwise he packs some pretty dangerous
moves that continuously damage your party. It may be a wise idea to bring
ranged/mage chrs into battle and let them duke it out with Held while you
destroy Faespheres.
-------------------- CONGRATULATIONS! YOU ARE AYATORIOUS! ---------------------

SITUATION BONUS [Defeated Held within 2 minutes.] yields a bonus reward of
MEMOIRS OF A MAGE.

-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-
CHAPTER #038 - LIBERATION
-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-

------------------------ HERE COMES A NEW CHALLENGER! -------------------------
Main Combatant/s: VERMIFIED HELD [60000 HP]           EXP: 8000    FOL: 3700
        ELEM-RES: Air:   0, Fire: 100, Earth: 100, Aether: 250, Water: 100
          SKILLS: Undyn
                  Spin Axis
                  Languo
                  Exgloto
                  Volt
                  Muto
                  Deadly Angle
                  AMBER LINK [105000 HP]
Side Combatant/s: FAESPHEREs [4000 HP]
Environmental hazard: none
------------------------------ GET READY! FIGHT! ----------------- Capell lv039
Kiriya and Savio join the battle as NPCs with infinite HP. Still, if everyone
on your team dies, it's Game Over, as Kiriya and Savio can't revive you.

Great! Not only do you have to bring down the boss, he's invisible. Play
Percipere near it to make him visible, then Aya Connect and start playing
Symphonic Blade on his cymballs.

Faespheres will keep popping up during the battle, so try to destroy them to
limit the damage Held can do to you. Otherwise he packs some pretty dangerous
moves that continuously damage your party. It may be a wise idea to bring
ranged/mage chrs into battle and let them duke it out with Held while you
destroy Faespheres.

Kiriya and Savio will keep Held busy most of the time, giving you ample chances
to stay away from them and heal your wounds. I was able to change skills on the
fly with ease.

Once you reduce Held's HP low enough, he'll keel over and barrier around the
link is gone. Run to it and start smacking. When Held recovers, barrier
reappears and knocks you back. The closer Held is to defeat, the faster the
barrier returns. Eventually Held croaks, and you can smack the link.
-------------------- CONGRATULATIONS! YOU ARE AYATORIOUS! ---------------------

Achievement <AMBER ACE> is yours!

===============================================================================
HALGITA
===============================================================================

Back in Halgita stuff happens. Go down to 1st floor and head for the exit to
Cobasna for a scene with Faina... leave the chapel and head for exit to Cobasna
for a scene with Genma.

-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-
CHAPTER #039 - MESSENGER OF PERIL
-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-

QUEST 31 COMPLETION - REPLICA KATANA
Edward Connect and check his IC menu. You'll see that a key item has been added
on the top - craft it to obtain REPLICA OF A KYLIN SWORD KI. Komachi Connect
and talk to Shido (2nd floor, E side) - hand over the replica to get HEROSONG.

QUEST 35 START & COMPLETION - THE THREE DOLLS
Talk to Faina and give her 3x Damask Cloth (Michelle can craft it at IC lv4).
Come back after 30 minutes to obtain CAPELL DOLL, FAINA DOLL, LEIF DOLL.

QUEST 36 START & COMPLETION - VERMIFORM HUNTER, STRIKE ONE
Touma Connect and talk to Shinkai in library on 2nd floor. He wants you to hunt
down at 10 vermiforms in Cobasna. This quest ties up nicely with next quest.
Venture into Cobasna and kill 10 vermiforms, then return to Halgita, Touma
Connect and talk to Shinkai to obtain LAUGHTER.

QUEST 37 START & COMPLETION - VERMIFORM HUNTER, STRIKE TWO
Talk to Sara, flower girl, on 1st floor. She wants you to examine vermiform's
remains for anything that could be used as info. Venture into Cobasna and head
for the spot where you fought Orthros. This time you'll find Vermiform here -
kill it to obtain BLOOD-STAINED SEAL KI. Return it to Sara for 50000 FOL.

Party needs to return to Fayel. Leave Halgita and head to Kolton.

===============================================================================
KOLTON
===============================================================================

Upon entering there will be a scene. Directly N from your position is entrance
to the palace. BEFORE YOU SEE THE KING, THERE IS A MISSABLE SCENE!

Walk over to N side of Kolton, where Michelle meets somebody, then enter the
church for some background on Michelle's past, and her Title 1 change.

QUEST 38 START & COMPLETION - SIMON'S CAUSE OF FATALITY
Talk to Oreg to learn about the culprit behind Simon's death. Now go talk to
Simon's grandparents and have some accusations fly your way. Return to Oreg for
more info, and you're asked to wait for official announcement.

Go see the king now.

-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-
CHAPTER #040 - AUDIENCE WITH THE KING
-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-

New chrs join the party: Kristofer joins as lv32 secondary chr, and comes
equipped with LONGBOW, LIZARD SKIN VEST, LIZARD SKIN CAP, LUX CLOGS. Seraphina
joins as lv32 secondardy chr, and comes equipped with "FEAR OF THE UNSEEN",
DAMASK GOWN, COTTON HAT, LUX SANDALS (my, you're pretty).

Explore the palace afterwards to get the know-around of the area. 1st floor has
nothing of interest, 2nd floor has meeting room to the N, and non-working
teleport pad to E. This is where you'll be able to enter bonus dungeon upon
completing the game. Hold onto your chocobos for a while longer.

QUEST 26 COMPLETION - COOK-OFF, PART 3
Aya Connect and talk to 'Senior apprentice' in NE house. She'll talk about the
tournament being cancelled and to contact you later. Hey, they didn't contact
me the second time! Talk to 'Master confectioner' to obtain WEDDING SPECIAL.

Talk to Kristofer for a scene about his past.

Kristofer Connect and talk to all female party members: Rucha, Komachi, Aya,
Seraphina, Dominica, and Michelle. When you're done with all six, Kristofer's
Trait 3 changes.
- Aya's scene will end with two choices.
  a) 'I think you should give up on her...
  b) '...Go ahead and give it a shot.'
- Dominica's scene is just laughing.
- Seraphina's scene ends with two choices.
  a) '...Not as popular with girls as you say?'
  b) '...The master of finding a date?'
- Komachi's scene is just laughing.
- Rucha's scene ends with two choices.
  a) 'You're so odd, Kristofer.'
  b) 'Well, that's just the way Kristofer is.'
- Michelle's scene ends with two choices.
  a) 'I'd show her my manly side.'
  b) 'I'd appeal to her maternal instincts.'

Talk to Touma to unlock Touma's Trait 4.

Savio Connect and talk to 'Seraphina's friend' on top floor of the castle.

Talk to Seraphina for a scene with choices to unlock Seraphina's Trait 3.
a) 'I'm not afraid because I have someone that I need.' <- ends the convo
b) 'I'm not afraid because someone needs me.' <- leads to c) and d)
c) 'Don't worry.' <- ends the convo
d) 'I need you, Seraphina.' <- leads to e) and f)
e) 'No one can replace you, Seraphina.' <- ends the convo
f) 'Yeah, you're right.' <- ends the convo

Seraphina Connect and talk to Michelle for change of Seraphina's Trait 2.

Board the ship to return to Zala.

===============================================================================
PORT ZALA
===============================================================================

After the scene save your game at the inn. And there's a lot of stuff to do
here...

Talk to Aya near the ship to obtain SUITE NOTATIONS KI.

Edward Connect and talk to Touma for a scene, after which you'll obtain
MEMOIRS OF A WARRIOR.

Vic Connect and talk to Komachi to unlock Komachi's Trait 3.

QUEST 23 CONTINUE - ZALA CLEAN-UP
Talk to Ivan in one of storage houses. He has mice problems... talk to him
again to hand over Tail in exchange for LUX BATON.

Kristofer Connect and talk to Michelle to change Kristofer's Trait 2.

Talk to Seraphina to change her Trait 3.

Eugene Connect and talk to Dominica to unlock Eugene's Palate.

QUEST 25 COMPLETION - FISHING WOES, PART 2
Savio Connect and talk to 'Fisherman' in bar. You'll obtain 2x CRAB MEAT,
3x DEVIANT FISH.

Rucha Connect and talk Rico for twins' quiz, which unlocks Rucha's Trait 3.
a) Q: Which one's a boy, Rico or Rucha?
   A: Rico.
b) Q: Who talked to Capell first, Rico or Rucha?
   A: Rico.
c) Q: Who likes looking at picture more than reading?
   A: Rucha.
d) Q: Who can talk to animals?
   A: Rico.
e) Q: Who do you like more, Rico or Rucha?
   A: You have three choices, first and second yield same reward, but third
      degrades your reward.
To sum up the rewards...
- for 0 (zero) correct answers you get RED BERRY POTION [RED BERRY]
- for 1 correct answer you get BLUE BERRY POTION [RED BERRY POTION]
- for 2 correct answers you get YELLOW BERRY POTION [BLUE BERRY POTION]
- for 3 correct answers you get GREEN BERRY POTION [YELLOW BERRY POTION]
- for 4 correct answers you get GOLD BERRY POTION [GREEN BERRY POTION]

We're done, leave for the dunes (there are new enemies present in the dunes,
and vermiforms as well) and leg it for Fayel.

===============================================================================
FAYEL
===============================================================================

QUEST 39 START & COMPLETION - MATILDA FROM HALGITA
If you recall, Matilda was babbling about having someone from Halgita with you.
Komachi Connect and talk to Matilda, then hand over Halgitian Jelly to receive
LOVEBIRD. If you don't have any, Aya can cook Halgitian Jelly on IC lv2.

Achievement is on the line, so save the game at the inn and enter the castle.
Ascend to 3rd floor and enter king's room...

-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-

TO FIGHT ENEMIES! SITUATION BONUS [Reached Sapran within 3 minutes.] will award
you bonus 30000 EXP! Additionally you'll receive achievement <MARATHON MAN>.

SAPRAN

Watch a bunch of scenes and bring a handkerchief.

-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-
CHAPTER #047 - PLEDGE
-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-

All playable chrs' traits and palates can be unlocked at this point (except
Komachi's Trait 4, which will be unlocked in next dungeon).

You start in 2nd floor of the castle. Go N to meeting room for another scene
with Svala, then exit the castle for a scene at the inn. Next chain has been
found at Castle Valette. To get there, take E exit of Kolton to the teleport
pad that usually leads to Cobasna. Well, it still leads there, only this time
you can choose another destination - Castle Valette.

Talk to Balbagan in the bar for some history on him.

Talk to Dominica in the inn for some history on her.

Talk to Kiriya in the general shop, choose between 'They really respect your
skills.' or 'You should forget about those idiots.', and Kiriya's Trait 3
changes.

QUEST 40 START & COMPLETION - SIMON, REST IN PIECES
Talk to Simon's grandparents and they'll apologize - MEMOIRS OF A KNIGHT is a
reward from granny. Finally, talk to Oreg to get 2x BLUE BERRY POTION,
2x PANACEA, MIRACULOUS MEDICINE.

Take the ship to Zala.

===============================================================================
PORT ZALA
===============================================================================

QUEST 41 START & COMPLETION - WAITRESS' WOES
Aya Connect and talk to waitress in the bar, then talk to barkeeper, then talk
to inn worker for PANACEA... talk to waitress again for SILVER FUR PUMPS.

QUEST 23 COMPLETION - ZALA CLEAN-UP
Aya Connect and talk to waitress in the bar, pick 'Yes.' and talk to her again
to hand over Strange-colored Bag. You'll score YELLOW BERRY POWDER.

Shlepp to Fayel.

===============================================================================
FAYEL
===============================================================================

QUEST 42 START & COMPLETION - SAMSON'S DEFEAT
Talk to 'Gossip-loving soldier' on the street, then Balbagan Connect and talk
to Samson in the castle. Samson lost a battle, and now he needs someone to get
revenge. Venture into the dunes and leg it for the oasis. In dead end to the E
you'll find a special Quezalcoatl, sporting 30000 HP. Skin it, return to Fayel,
Balbagan Connect and talk to Samson to receive BLAZE AXE.

QUEST 43 START & COMPLETION - EMMIE'S LOVE TROUBLES
Aya Connect and talk to Emmie in throne room. You'll need to set her up with a
guy from the Force. Connect with every guy on your team and bring him to Emmie.
Those are: Edward, Eugene, Balbagan, Savio, Kiriya, Touma, and Kristofer. After
you bring seventh guy, talk to Emmie again to obtain MYSTERIOUS MEDICINE.
Here's the biggest catch of them all - Emmie likes Vic! As Sirian_Hawk put it:
"Someone didn't get the memo!"

QUEST 44 START & COMPLETION - GIRLS OF FAYEL ARE THE STRONGEST (I agree!)
Dominica Connect and talk to 'Aspiring warrior' kid near the entrance of Fayel.
If he says about Dominica being warrior of Fayel and stuff about Wendigo,
you've triggered the quest. Go into the dunes and take a right to end up in a
spot where you rescued Gustav earlier in the game. You'll encounter a Wendigo
with 55000 HP. Take it out and return to Fayel - Dominica Connect and talk to
the stupid kid to obtain POLEAXE.

===============================================================================
BURGUSSTADT
===============================================================================

QUEST 45 START & COMPLETION - ROOKIE'S LOVE TROUBLES
Talk to 'Rookie soldier' in the castle, choose 'Sure.' twice and get
RING FOR DELIVERY KI. You can talk to other soldiers walking around for clues
on who he likes. When you get to restricted area (SW corner), and considering
you're facing them, it's the left of the two girl guards. BLUE BERRY POWDER is
your reward.

This is also a good time to hunt down all locked and out-of-reach chests we've
been skipping. Head on to Nolaan.

===============================================================================
NOLAAN
===============================================================================

Komachi Connect and open locked SCH in twins' house for 50000 FOL.

===============================================================================
GRAAD WOODS
===============================================================================

Keep walking until you get to the bridge. Komachi Connect and Honeysuckle BSCH
in the stream for CHARMING PERFUME.

===============================================================================
LUCE PLAINS
===============================================================================

Walk to middle of the plains, Komachi Connect and Honeysuckle BSCH atop one of
the pillars for MEMOIRS OF A THIEF. On E side of the plains is trapped WCH with
750 FOL (poison trap). Locked SCH with BLUE BERRY POTION can be found on W side
of the plains.

===============================================================================
ORADIAN DUNES
===============================================================================

Komachi Connect and Honeysuckle BSCH for MEMOIRS OF AN ALCHEMIST in the pond of
the oasis. Additionally, open locked SCH in remains of the house to obtain
EAGLE EYE. One more to loot - go to Zala's entrance and turn around. As you
walk S, pay attention to your left and spot BSCH on a stone arch above. Komachi
Connect and Honeysuckle it for MEMOIRS OF A KNIGHT.

===============================================================================
BIHAR MINES
===============================================================================

Take the entrance near Zala. When you turn S round the corner, you'll see a
portion of the wall missing with lava behind. Take a peek to spot BSCH in the
rocks. Komachi Connect and Honeysuckle it for MERCURIUS METAL. Walk over to the
entrance from Oradian Mountains, turn around and open locked SCH in first N
room for BLAZE METAL.

===============================================================================
ORADIAN MOUNTAINS
===============================================================================

Enter via Bihar Mines. Climb a bit to end up in open area with several rocks
protruding out the ground. On top of one of these is BSCH with DRAGON HIDE -
Komachi Connect and Honeysuckle it.

Now climb to entrance of Vesplume, then turn around and go E to end up in dead
end with rocks protruding out (same area you found Aya's bow in one of earlier
quests). Komachi Connect and Honeysuckle BSCH for MEMOIRS OF A HUNTER (located
on one of those rocks).

Finally, descend towards Fayel and take the exit which spits you out next to
the palace. On a small ledge open locked SCH with YELLOW BERRY POWDER.

===============================================================================
FAYEL
===============================================================================

Komachi Connect and open locked SCH in Aya's room for CHARMING PERFUME, then
another locked SCH in emir's room for 20000 FOL.

===============================================================================
PORT ZALA
===============================================================================

Komachi Connect and open locked SCH in the inn for PREMIUM KARATHOS, and
another locked SCH in first Zala's house for 15000 FOL.

===============================================================================
ZALAN COAST
===============================================================================

Komachi Connect and Honeysuckle BSCH from the sea for MEMOIRS OF A WARRIOR.

===============================================================================
COBASNA TIMBERLANDS
===============================================================================

Yeah, there's two chests I haven't yet collected. Enter from Kolton, then go E,
N at the cross, N at the cross, E at the cross, take the warp. Turn W, and nail
WCH with EBONY WOOD, then E, N at the cross, and you're at the clearing of
Orthros battle earlier in the game. Follow the purple lights emanating from the
ground until you come to forest stream. Komachi Connect and Honeysuckle BSCH in
the nearby pond for LOVEBIRD.

Make your party Capell, Aya, Komachi and Rucha. Then check your items to see if
you're stocked on revival items, and status-curing items (especially charm!).
Head to Valette. KOMACHI IS MANDATORY CHR! Else kiss your Compulsive
achievement goodbye.

-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-
CHAPTER #048 - SIEGE
-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-

===============================================================================
CASTLE VALETTE - ONE-TIME-ONLY-AREA!
===============================================================================

Make three parties - party A Capell, Aya, Komachi and Rucha, party B whoever,
party C whoever, but make sure they're full, okay?

As soon as you arrive, teleporter goes kaputt. Kill all enemies, then walk N,
killing enemies as you go - every level you gain will be worth it, so do kill
everything.

Second chamber you'll reach has MCH in NW corner (it's Iron Box Mimic), and
locked SCH in NE corner with MIRACULOUS MEDICINE. Follow the path to third
chamber, where you'll see some undead bozo spawn a bunch of skeletons. You need
to shatter them all to continue forward.

Follow the path further to 1stcross, take E path. There's a blue door with an
orb above it - it flashes red and blue. Aya Connect and Ravaging Raptor the orb
when it's glowing blue. This will unlock the door, otherwise you'll be ambushed
if you strike it when it's red. Inside the niche open three WCH for 1000 FOL,
5000 FOL, 3000 FOL. Read the blue writing on the wall that says "The road lined
in crimson spirals to demise. Feed you desire following the azure way.". We
already figured it out the hard way... Back to 1stcross and take S path to
fourth chamber.

E path from fourth chamber is dead end, so take N path to fifth chamber. In
this chamber you have two further paths - N one leads to a small room with blue
door and an orb above it. Aya Connect and Ravaging Raptor it when it's glowing
blue to open the door. Komachi Connect and open three locked SCH for
FEATHER WRISTBAND, VIPER FANG, GLACIAL DELIGHT. Back to fifth chamber and take
E path to 2ndcross.

WUPAZZ comments: If you deliberately shoot the wrong color of the orb, this
will spawn Dancing Crossbows and Flying Swords. Crossbows may rarely drop
Placidus Wood, which you'll need for upcoming IC writing upgrade quest.

Continue S to a dead end with BSCH with MEMOIRS OF A MAGE, back to 2ndcross and
fill your HP/MP. Take E path into sixth chamber for a skeleton army massacre. N
path leads to a small room with blue door and an orb above it. Aya Connect and
Ravaging Raptor it when it's glowing blue to open the door. Open two WCH for
JUNK, CRYSTALLITE METAL, and BSCH for MEMOIRS OF A THIEF. Back to sixth chamber
and take E path into seventh chamber.

Go downstairs for next skelly massacre, then top your HP/MP. A boss is coming
up as soon as you step out of the underground tunnel located in seventh
chamber. Set your tactics to 'Save MP', and ensure your party can use Maiden's
Scorn to cure charmed chrs.

------------------------ HERE COMES A NEW CHALLENGER! -------------------------
Main Combatant/s: ENVY [230000 HP]                    EXP: 8200    FOL: 4000
        ELEM-RES: Air: 250, Fire: 100, Earth:  50, Aether: 100, Water: 250
          SKILLS: Sword Dance
                  Astrobeam
                  Invoke Spirits
                  Amoro
                  Deadly Words
Side Combatant/s: RIB FORAGERs [10000 HP], SKULL SOLDIERs, SKULL KNIGHTs
Environmental hazard: none
------------------------------ GET READY! FIGHT! ----------------- Capell lv045
Stand your ground for a while, removing skellies as they pop up. Eventually
other two parties will arrive for a huuuge festival fest with fireworks and
more babes you can shake your stick at! Get your mind out of the gutter, you!

Charmed chrs will regain senses soon due to Maiden's Scorn usage. I suggest
setting Reginleif and Cutting Gavotte as Capell's battle skills. Use Gavotte
frequently as it can mow down multiple targets. So can Regin, but it has longer
activation time for the trade-off in thousands of damage.
-------------------- CONGRATULATIONS! YOU ARE AYATORIOUS! ---------------------

Exit S into 8th chamber with SPN. Cool! Head S and read the writing on the wall
that says "The crimson flame engulfs the alabaster bird, Which ever-hungry
feeds on azure skies, Clouds that cover amber lands, sealing in, Onyx seas
whose waters quench wild fire. Repeat the cycle to weave the path together."

Confusing, is it not? By looking it up in the dictionary these are the meanings
of colors: crimson is red, azure is blue, alabaster is white, amber is yellow,
and onyx is purple. Once you logically put together the colors and wording of
the puzzle, you get this order - red, white, blue, yellow, purple, red, white,
blue, yellow, purple, red, white, blue, yellow, purple, the end.

So beginning from the spot in front of the blue writing... take the door to S
(note red circle on the ground, denoting cycle has started), white door to E,
blue door to S, yellow door to S, purple door to W, red door to W, white door
to N, blue door to W, yellow door to W, purple door to S, red door to S, white
door to E, blue door to S, yellow door to E, purple door to S. SITUATION BONUS
[Solved Chamber of Elements with no mistakes.] will fully recover your HP and
MP.

Enter ninth chamber and smash enemies lurking nearby, then wait for one of
other parties to clear the enemies from catwalk above. Notice a chest up there
as well? That's why we have Komachi - Komachi Connect and Honeysuckle BSCH for
INSTRUMENTAL SWORD. Walk to SW end of ninth chamber for passage leading S to
tenth chamber, W to 11th chamber, N to 12th chamber... hmmm, MCH (turns into
Iron Box Mimic) with plenty of gil, then walk W into 13th chamber.

Just before you step into 14th chamber, read the writing on the wall that says
"The road lined in crimson spirals to demise. Feed you desire following the
azure way. The future is framed in emerald light." - oh noes... Crimson is red,
and that is bad. Azure is blue, and that is good. Emerald is green, and it
opens the path forward.

You have two crystals in 14th chamber - their colors glow in specific order of
blue, green, red, blue, green, red, and so on. Strike either crystal when it's
blue, and then strike the other crystal when it's blue as well. You need to be
somewhat quick, otherwise the colors of striked crystal will begin cycling
again. Smacking two blues will open S door, leading to a room with two WCH with
40000 FOL, 6550 FOL, and BSCH with MEMOIRS OF A HUNTER. Then smack two greens
to open W door into 15th chamber.

Smacking two blues opens N door into a room with three WCH with
RACHNUVUS CLOTH, CAPRICCIO NOTATIONS KI, RACHNUVUS SHELL. Then smack two greens
to open W door into 16th chamber.

Ugh, can it be more obvious? Play Percipere near orb stands (familiar sound
source) to make two crystals appear. Smacking two blues opens S door into a
room with three WCH with BLAZE METAL, BLAZE METAL, SALAMANDER SKIN. Then smack
two greens to open W door into a long corridor, which eventually leads to the
boss. I suggest returning to SPN to save your progress - you can walk through
that darn Chamber of Elements without harm now.

Whether or not you decide to go save, proceed down the corridor until you find
another door. Top your HP/MP and enter...

------------------------ HERE COMES A NEW CHALLENGER! -------------------------
Main Combatant/s: SARANDA [250000 HP]                 EXP: ????    FOL: 4100
        ELEM-RES: Air:  50, Fire:  50, Earth:  50, Aether:  50, Water:  50
          SKILLS: Whipflash
                  Aerial Arc
                  Hydrill
                  Pyrgeddon
                  Parallel Darkness
                  ASHEN LINK [150000 HP]
Side Combatant/s: none
Environmental hazard: none
------------------------------ GET READY! FIGHT! ----------------- Capell lv046
Run around for a while so that reinforcements arrive in form of one of your
teams. They act as NPCs, have infi-HP and cannot die, but same can't be said
for your team. If everyone is KOed, it's Game Over, so tread with caution. I
found it best to let my other chrs and NPCs smash Saranda around, while tapping
Y for healing requests. Ocassionally I'd run and touch Saranda with Gavotte or
Regin.

Once you reduce Saranda's HP low enough, she'll keel over and barrier around
the link is gone. Run to it and start smacking. When Saranda recovers, barrier
reappears and knocks you back. The closer Saranda is to defeat, the faster the
barrier returns. Eventually Saranda croaks, and you can smack the link.
-------------------- CONGRATULATIONS! YOU ARE AYATORIOUS! ---------------------

Achievement <ASHEN ASSAILANT> is unlocked.

-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-
CHAPTER #049 - TO CASANDRA
-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-

===============================================================================
PLODHIF CAVERNS
===============================================================================
Has 1 Cracked Rock.

Go W, talk to Genma to rest or buy supplies, save at SPN, and follow the path.
Once you walk near some water puddles, Komachi Connect and Honeysuckle BSCH for
MERCURIUS METAL. Further W and a scene occurs, where Capell is cut from others
by a giant centipede.

Try to avoid the centipede, N, open WCH for CRYSTALLITE METAL, then follow the
path until dead end. Aya and others are to your right, out of reach, but
remember that chest you see. Try to avoid the centipede, and it'll destroy the
wall opening your path further.

Follow your nose until you end at a clearing with a chest and a spider
(centipede suddenly busting outta right wall scared me). Michelle will help you
destroy the spider, then open trapped WCH for RED BERRY POWDER (dwindle trap).
Remember the chest on the ledge where Michelle is.

Walk S into big cavern system. At 1stcross go SW for another two paths, both
leading to dead ends - one has a spider, the other locked chest and familiar
sound... play Percipere to uncover BSCH with MYSTERIOUS MEDICINE. Return to
1stcross and take E path. The rest of this part of cavern doesn't have anything
else interesting, except one more thing - at E end you'll hear that familiar
sound. Play Percipere to dissipate the wall and discover part of cavern with
MCH (Iron Box Mimic) and BSCH with 160000 FOL (wow).

The path that'll take further is found in SE part - it'll take you downward
some into a corridor with some stalactites. Sheathe your sword and stick to S
side of the corridor. Open trapped WCH for WHITE BERRY POTION (paralysis trap)
and continue hugging S side. That stupid centipede will charge from front and
miss you.

Follow the path for a scene of party being reunited. Make sure your party
includes Komachi, save at SPN and retrace your steps to NE of SPN to claim
contents of three chests we left back there.

Locked SCH has RACHNUVUS CLOTH, then Komachi Connect and Honeysuckle those two
BSCH for GENIUS' QUILL, MERCENARY HELMET. Return to SPN, save your game, and
take W exit. I also advise spamming enemies within the caverns until Capell
reaches lv50 at which point he learns Grinn Valesti.

===============================================================================
PIERIA MARSHLANDS
===============================================================================
Has 1 Cracked Rock.

Komachi Connect and Honeysuckle BSCH for ATLANTIS METAL, then go E.

------------------------ HERE COMES A NEW CHALLENGER! -------------------------
Main Combatant/s: DRAGON [160000 HP]                  EXP: ????    FOL: ????
        ELEM-RES: Air: 100, Fire: -50, Earth: 100, Aether: 100, Water: 250
Side Combatant/s: MANTIFISHes, MOSS GLUTTONs, BLUE DROGO WARRIORs
Environmental hazard: none
------------------------------ GET READY! FIGHT! ----------------- Capell lv050
When battle starts, retreat to SW end of the field. This not only reduces the
amount of reinforcements dragon will be getting, it also avoids chests to be
destroyed.

Kill any enemies that may have followed you, and patiently wait for the boss to
stop flying and to come down to the ground. Be on the move to avoid damage from
Flame Cone. When it's grounded, assault the boss mercilessly, and tap Y every
so often. Also take care to remove sidekicks if any spawn.
-------------------- CONGRATULATIONS! YOU ARE AYATORIOUS! ---------------------

I highly highly recommend that you attempt to win with situ-bonus. Dragon Eye
is a very rare treasure for Seraphic Gate, and winning one now will save you
some grief for later.

SITUATION BONUS [Defeated the dragon within 2 minutes.] yields a reward of
DRAGON EYE, DRAGON FANG. After the battle Komachi Connect and open trapped WCH
for GLUTTON HIDE (dwindle trap), trapped WCH for PIUS WOOD (bomb trap) and open
three locked SCH for MYSTERIOUS MEDICINE, CASANDRA BANAPPLE, DRAGON EYE. Exit N
for a scene.

-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-
CHAPTER #050 - TOGETHER
-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-

After several scenes Split and Aya make up. *tied Capell and disposed of him*
I'm Aya's Man now.

Ahem... party of Capell and Aya. Familiar sound behind you, eh? Play Percipere
to uncover BSCH with DRAGON HIDE. Before you go downstairs to that SPN, check
to your S - there's a teleport pad back to Kolton, though it's inactive at the
moment. Save at SPN, then walk E for a scene. Make your party of Capell, Aya,
Rucha and Komachi (my favorites) and return to Kolton's warp. There's also
Genma for restocking on provisions or free resting.

Should you need to do anything in Kolton or the rest of the world, now's the
last chance to do so.

Kent P. comments: Before you head into the Underwater Palace you can take the
teleporter back to Kolton. The reason you would want to do this is because this
is the first time available you are able to upgrade your IC abilities. You can
talk to Kristopher in Kolton and answer his question to upgrade Blacksmithing,
for instance. This will enable you to create very powerful equipment that will
make the Underwater Palace much, much easier.

Once you leave for Underwater Palace, you aren't coming back until you beat the
game. Add Balbagan to party, then leave to Pieria.

Walk towards the entrance to Plodhif, and before you arrive at the place of
battle against the dragon, you'll spot a cracked rock. Balbagan Connect and
Gigatackle the rock, then open BSCH for WHITE BERRY POWDER. Go to Plodhif now.

===============================================================================
PLODHIF CAVERNS
===============================================================================

Race to SPN area, Balbagan Connect and Gigatackle the cracked rock, then open
BSCH for EMPYREAN CLOTH. Go to Pieria now and return to Kolton.

===============================================================================
KOLTON
===============================================================================

QUEST 46 START & COMPLETION - IC BLACKSMITH UPGRADE
Talk to Kristofer for a question. Choose 'I'll try it.', then pick the answer
'It's B>A>C in that order.'. Now you can forge amazing new items! Even if you
get it wrong, you can answer as many times as you want.

Woodchuck your way to Halgita.

===============================================================================
HALGITA
===============================================================================

QUEST 47 START & COMPLETION - IC COOKING UPGRADE
Talk to Rucha for a scene. She got this ancient recipe and wants you to bring
her some stuff: SLICED RARE SALMON, 2x PREHISTORIC MEAT, 3x PIERIA MUSHROOM,
3x SAPRAN GREEN PEPPER. Give her these items... Now you can cook amazing new
foods!

Note that all but rare salmon can be bought - you can get Sliced Rare Salmon
from Mantifish enemy in Seraphic Gate, or in Pieria Marshlands (thanks for the
tip to WUPAZZ).

Sail to Zala next.

===============================================================================
PORT ZALA
===============================================================================

QUEST 48 START - IC WRITING UPGRADE
Talk to Rico for a scene. He got this ancient paper which refuses to be written
upon. Rico wants you to bring him some stuff: 2x Clerk's Quill (you need
Placidus Wood, which can be gotten from Seraphic Gate), Genius's Quill,
2x Lunatite, Amarlista.

Let the wind take you to Fayel.

FAYEL
===============================================================================

QUEST 49 START & COMPLETION - IC ALCHEMY UPGRADE
Go to Savio's room in the castle and talk to Alchemeister for a scene. Give him
Dragon Eye... Now you alchemy skills have been improved!

Last place of interest is Sapran.

SAPRAN

QUEST 50 START & COMPLETION - IC ENCHANTMENT UPGRADE
Descend to chain's base in N part of village and talk to elder for a little
quiz. Answers are...
a) During a new moon.
b) Levan.
c) Bone Comb.
d) Burgusstadt.
e) Faina.
Enchantment powers have increased!

That's it, leave for Pieria.

PIERIA MARSHLANDS

Pass the place of dragon battle (or return to Kolton to get rid of Balbagan if

-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-
CHAPTER #051 - PALACE BOUND
-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-

Are you ready? You will have to smash thru four bosses before you get a chance
to save, so doublecheck your inventory. Step into the teleporter for the palace
and let final assault begin!

===============================================================================
UNDERWATER PALACE
===============================================================================

Walk E for a scene...

-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-
CHAPTER #052 - SHOWDOWN
-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-

------------------------ HERE COMES A NEW CHALLENGER! -------------------------
Main Combatant/s: ISKAN DU BAL [350000 HP]            EXP: ????    FOL: ????
        ELEM-RES: Air: 100, Fire: 100, Earth: 250, Aether: 100, Water:  50
          SKILLS: Heraldic Edge
                  False Regalia
                  Crestfallen
                  [Jumping slash + downward slash + sideslash combo]
Side Combatant/s: none
Environmental hazard: none
------------------------------ GET READY! FIGHT! ----------------- Capell lv051
Most of Bal's attacks are telegraphed long enough for you to get out of the
way... which you should or face fearsome damage. Getting behind Iskan's back is
often times best medicine to avoid his attacks, except for uppercut slash jump,
and forward slash which ends with a shockwave.

I usually pointed Capell behind Iskan while he was charging one of his moves
and spammed Regin on his ass until he bit the dust. Don't forget tapping Y for
healing requests, as other party members are sure to be taking a beating.
-------------------- CONGRATULATIONS! YOU ARE AYATORIOUS! ---------------------

SITUATION BONUS [Didn't finish off Iskan via Capell.] yields extra 35000 EXP!

After scenes have ended, make three parties - my party A was Capell, Aya, Rucha
and Komachi. Walk E and sniff behind the warp pad for BSCH with SOLAR NECKLACE,
then hop into the warp.

1ST FLOOR

The rest of the dungeon is extremely straightforward. You basically just follow
your nose, opening doors as you go, and defeating a set of enemies in order to
unlock the way further, then collecting the chest, and hopping into warp to
next floor. Your foes on this floor are several Fountain Beaks and two Garms.
Reward is BSCH with FEEBLE CAPE.

2ND FLOOR

This is a boss floor.

------------------------ HERE COMES A NEW CHALLENGER! -------------------------
Main Combatant/s: 2x VELD THE EVIL EYE [120000 HP]    EXP: 5200    FOL: 3900
        ELEM-RES: Air:   0, Fire:  50, Earth:  50, Aether: 100, Water:  50
          SKILLS: Volt
                  Somnio
Side Combatant/s: none
Environmental hazard: none
------------------------------ GET READY! FIGHT! ----------------- Capell lv052
Not very different from Kron way back in Vesplume Tower, except more HP and
there being two of them. They love to warp thus making you waste MP for missed
attacks, but you'll get them in the long run. Healthy supply of status recovery
items will keep you going until both bastids are history.
-------------------- CONGRATULATIONS! YOU ARE AYATORIOUS! ---------------------

Reward in BSCH is PHOENIX FEATHER JACKET.

3RD FLOOR

A couple of Order Experts, Order Sorceresses, Order Officers, Order Snipers,
and Frost Gigases are here to meet you. Prize from BSCH is FEEBLE WRISTBAND.

4TH FLOOR

This is a boss floor.

------------------------ HERE COMES A NEW CHALLENGER! -------------------------
Main Combatant/s: TARASQUE [167250 HP]                EXP: 5200    FOL: 4000
        ELEM-RES: Air: 100, Fire: -50, Earth: 100, Aether: 100, Water: 250
          SKILLS: Snakesnap
                  Charge
Side Combatant/s: none
Environmental hazard: none
------------------------------ GET READY! FIGHT! ----------------- Capell lv053
This is not a hard battle, as Orthros has only two moves: Snakesnap for
continuous flame damage around it, and Charge for physical damage. I was having
Capell stand just out of reach of flame spewing and spammed Regin until Tar
went into history.
-------------------- CONGRATULATIONS! YOU ARE AYATORIOUS! ---------------------

No rewards from chests this time.

5TH FLOOR

You'll face some Queen Wasps and two Lava Gluttons. Reward from BSCH is
PHOENIX FEATHER HOOD.

6TH FLOOR

This is a boss floor.

------------------------ HERE COMES A NEW CHALLENGER! -------------------------
Main Combatant/s: GREED [277777 HP]                   EXP: 5700    FOL: 4000
        ELEM-RES: Air: 250, Fire: 100, Earth:  50, Aether: 100, Water: 100
          SKILLS: Sword Dance
                  Astrobeam
                  Invoke Spirits
                  Amoro
                  Deadly Words
Side Combatant/s: FLYING SWORDs, RIB FORAGERs [18000 HP], SKULL WARRIORs
Environmental hazard: none
------------------------------ GET READY! FIGHT! ----------------- Capell lv054
Greed is same as its Envy pal - it'll often summon Ribs to act as a shield for
it, and they can also be used as a very potent and dangerous move Sword Dance.
Hence I recommend spamming Grinn or Regin on Greed, with former being much more
efficient as it's faster and covers wider area. Don't forget Y button.
-------------------- CONGRATULATIONS! YOU ARE AYATORIOUS! ---------------------

Reward from BSCH is PHOENIX FEATHER BOOTS.

7TH FLOOR

Finally SPN, and Genma's usual service of rest or buying provisions. BSCH has
AMARLISTA inside.

8TH FLOOR

This is a boss floor.

------------------------ HERE COMES A NEW CHALLENGER! -------------------------
Main Combatant/s: KRAKEN [287250 HP]                  EXP: 5200    FOL: 4000
        ELEM-RES: Air: 100, Fire: 100, Earth: 250, Aether: 100, Water: -50
          SKILLS: Spearlord
                  Ink Blast
                  [Tentacle swipe]
                  Whiplash
Side Combatant/s: none
Environmental hazard: none
------------------------------ GET READY! FIGHT! ----------------- Capell lv054
Whee, a new boss foe, not a recycled one! Fairly easy boss, stay behind its
back and use Grinn or Regin until it falls. Be ready to take some damage when
it uses a move which damages everyone around the boss, and heal afterwards.
-------------------- CONGRATULATIONS! YOU ARE AYATORIOUS! ---------------------

BSCH award is SOVEREIGNTY RING. If you want, return to 7th floor to save your
game - there are two more bosses to plow thru before next SPN.

9TH FLOOR

Walk forth and hold onto your closest babes! Fix up some favorite party and off
I go.

------------------------ HERE COMES A NEW CHALLENGER! -------------------------
Main Combatant/s: KARATHOS [250000 HP]                EXP: 8000    FOL: 5000
        ELEM-RES: Air: 100, Fire: 100, Earth: 250, Aether: 100, Water: -50
          SKILLS: Killer Bite
                  Poison Rain
                  Jet Spin
Side Combatant/s: none
Environmental hazard: none
------------------------------ GET READY! FIGHT! ----------------- Capell lv055
Stay behind its back and use Grinn or Regin. Frontal attacks are not
recommended because of very high attack power of Kar's bites. It'll often KO a
chr, so you're likely to burn thru some revival items. When it decides to start
spinning around, seek cover behind pillars or stay close to outer perimeter (or
if you time your parry just right, you can stop it).

Steve F. comments: The way I did it was to let Karathos target Capell with it's
Bite attack annd then run around it so that it has to turn to attack. If you
run to its back leg, hit it normally a couple of times and then run behind it
again, it will never attack, only keep turning around until it's in range
(which shouldn't happen) or dead.
-------------------- CONGRATULATIONS! YOU ARE AYATORIOUS! ---------------------

Boss spits out KARATHOS HELMET when smoked.

------------------------ HERE COMES A NEW CHALLENGER! -------------------------
Main Combatant/s: DINOEL [300000 HP]                  EXP: ????    FOL: ????
        ELEM-RES: Air: 100, Fire: 100, Earth:  50, Aether: 100, Water:  50
          SKILLS: XIIIth Word
                  VIIth Violation
                  ZERO Revolution
                  [Whip-shoot + sideswipe combo]
                  Geoclaw
Side Combatant/s: CHAINSPIKEs
Environmental hazard: none
------------------------------ GET READY! FIGHT! ----------------- Capell lv055
Din is surrounded by six Chainspikes, which need to be destroyed. Grinn is a
perfect offensive move for that, and Din can be attacked after all are
destroyed.

He has a couple of dangerous moves in arsenal - shooting out a whip in straight
direction, then slashing with it twice; XIIIth Word which makes several chains
protrude from ground below your chrs; VIIth Violation which makes chains appear
on his back and start swaying back and forth damaging everyone they touch
(parry these to stun him); and finally ZERO Revolution - big energy ball, which
deals extreme damage when it hits the ground.

Rucha and Aya were dealing good amounts of ranged damage with their arrows and
spells, while Komachi and Capell took care of close quarters business. Keep on
Y button as well - don't neglect healing.
-------------------- CONGRATULATIONS! YOU ARE AYATORIOUS! ---------------------

SITUATION BONUS [Didn't finish off Dinoel via Capell.] yields extra 40000 EXP!
You also get an achievement <VENGEANCE AT LAST>.

-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-
CHAPTER #053 - UNENDING FIGHT
-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-

WARNING! WHAT YOU SEE BEFORE YOU IS THE FINAL SAVE POINT OF THE GAME! WARNING!

After you defeat the last boss, you'll be able to make Clear Game Save. When
you load this particular save data, you'll be returned just to the point before
entering Underwater Palace.

Save your game at SPN. If you need recovery items, return to 7th floor and
restock at Genma's.

Walk W, open the door and go upstairs for some scenes of getting access to
final... dungeon, so to speak.

-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-
CHAPTER #054 - LUNAR PASSAGE
-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-

Sit back, grab some chips and enjoy the scenes.

-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-
CHAPTER #055 - TO THE STARS
-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-

===============================================================================
LUNAR SANCTUARY
===============================================================================

Nothing special, keep walking N. Final challengers, here we go!

-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-
CHAPTER #056 - HUBRIS OF [SPOILER]
-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-

------------------------ HERE COMES A NEW CHALLENGER! -------------------------
Main Combatant/s: DINOEL [300000 HP]                  EXP: 11000   FOL: 6000
        ELEM-RES: Air: 100, Fire: 100, Earth:  50, Aether: 100, Water:  50
          SKILLS: XIIIth Word
                  VIIth Violation
                  ZERO Revolution
                  [Whip-shoot + sideswipe combo]
                  Geoclaw
Side Combatant/s: none
Environmental hazard: none
------------------------------ GET READY! FIGHT! ----------------- Capell lv056
Din isn't very different from last battle (more HP and higher stats, though),
and has same moves in arsenal - shooting out a whip in straight direction, then
slashing with it twice; XIIIth Word which makes several chains protrude from
ground below your chrs; VIIth Violation which makes chains appear on his back
and start swaying back and forth damaging everyone they touch (parry these to
stun him); and finally ZERO Revolution, which involves powering up a big energy
ball, which deals extreme damage when it hits the ground.

Rucha and Aya were dealing good amounts of ranged damage with their arrows and
spells, while Komachi and Capell took care of close quarters business. Keep on
Y button as well - don't neglect healing.
-------------------- CONGRATULATIONS! YOU ARE AYATORIOUS! ---------------------

SITUATION BONUS [Defeated Dinoel within 2 minutes.] yields AMARLISTA reward.

Bla bla bla... come on down, bastard. I'll teach you some manners.

------------------------ HERE COMES A NEW CHALLENGER! -------------------------
Main Combatant/s: FINAL BOSS [100000 HP]              EXP: 13500   FOL: 1000
        ELEM-RES: Air: 100, Fire: 100, Earth: 100, Aether: 100, Water: 100
          SKILLS: [Summon meteors]
Side Combatant/s: 6x NETHERMYRMIDONs [42000 HP]       EXP: ---     FOL: ---
        ELEM-RES: Air: 100, Fire: 100, Earth: 100, Aether: 100, Water: 100
          SKILLS: Broken Moon (green)
                  Crescent Reign
                  2x SUPERNHELOTs [68000 HP]          EXP: ---     FOL: ---
                  Fanatic Lunaseer
                  [Fireball + lightning ball combo]
                  [Light beam]
        ELEM-RES: Air: 100, Fire: 100, Earth: 100, Aether: 100, Water: 100
Environmental hazard: none
------------------------------ GET READY! FIGHT! ----------------- Capell lv056
Y button - my best friend, after Aya, of course.

Boss is surrounded by six Nethers. These must fall before boss himself steps
onto the field, trying to level your party. And boy, will he be doing that...
at least 50x Miraculous Medicine is recommended to have, in addition to
Seraphinaload of recovery items, because magic healing will hardly keep up the
pace.

You must not strike Nethers that are spinning, but can dish damage to those
that are not spinning. Grinn, sick 'em! His most dangerous moves during this
stage are summoning of your clones (try facing lv255 chrs!), a spinning storm,
and gas-type attack which causes all sorts of status ailments.

Once Nethers are history, couple of Supers become a target. Use Regin or Grinn
to attack from distance, then retreat. Boss will summon six fire balls which
can home in on your position, then they burn for some continuous damage. When
they're done, they change into lightning balls while trying to draw you closer
by force. Fanatic Lunaseer is an attack where boss creates a couple of lasers
circling the ground around him. Finally, he sometimes makes light appear behind
him - don't get close or you'll take continuous damage. Once you also destroy
both Supers, party time.

Boss will now begin moving around and start summoning small meteors on the
battlefield in wide circle around him. Continuous melee damage is very
dangerous to consider right now, cos multiple meteors can toss you around until
you're KOed. Wait for meteors to stop raining, then quickly move in, smack him
twice or thrice, and move back out. Repeat until he's gone.
-------------------- CONGRATULATIONS! YOU ARE AYATORIOUS! ---------------------

Achievement <DEICIDE> is unlocked.

===============================================================================
===============================================================================
08.)                         SERAPHIC GATE - G0800
===============================================================================
===============================================================================

When you load 'Clear Data' save, you'll appear at SPN in Pieria Marshlands.
Take the warp behind you back to Kolton and enter the palace. Climb to 2nd
floor and check E room. Warp pad here is now active and will take you to
Seraphic Gate.

GAME'S FOREWORD -=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-
Welcome to the Seraphic Gate!

The creatures lurking within these halls are the foulest and fiercest you have
ever known. Balls of steel are required. ...But titanium is recommended.

To help match the power of your foes, item creation and enchantment has been
enhanced. There is also powerful equipment awaiting you on each floor. Take
advantage of it, and good luck reaching the bottom.

You can return to the world above via the teleporter at the entrance.
-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=- GAME'S FOREWORD

SPLIT'S FOREWORD =-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-
Komachi is required to get some treasures with Honeysuckle, and Balbagan to
bash some rocks. Mare Lunaris song by Capell as well. Don't forget to take a
healer along!

SG houses quite a few unique weapons which you cannot get anywhere else. It's
also the place for repeatedly skinning enemies for some tough-to-obtain
materials, like Dragon Eyes and Feeble Cloths.

You will eventually encounter a bonus chr who can join your party, but you have
to kick his ass first by soloing him with Capell. I'll tell you when the time
is right to be prepared.

Before you venture into SG, have Kristofer make Karathos Wristbands for
everybody on the bench so that they can gain full 100% EXP from foes, instead
of crappy 50%.

Minimap and map aren't available in SG, so you'll have to remember the way.

Pick your favorite party and let's go!
-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-= SPLIT'S FOREWORD

===============================================================================
SERAPHIC GATE, FLOOR #01 - GRAAD PRISON
===============================================================================
ENEMIES                 | HP
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Blue Drogo Warrior      | 17000
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Larva                   | 7000
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Tiger Rachnuvus         | 20000
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Vembert (BOSS)          | 340000
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Path is simple - only downstairs. Eventually you'll encounter Fatass Vembert.

------------------------ HERE COMES A NEW CHALLENGER! -------------------------
Main Combatant/s: VEMBERT [340000 HP]                 EXP: 14000   FOL: 10000
        ELEM-RES: Air: 100, Fire:-100, Earth: 100, Aether: 150, Water: 250
          SKILLS: Brandishbane
                  [Smack]
                  [Smack + axe strike combo]
Side Combatant/s: none
Environmental hazard: none
------------------------------ GET READY! FIGHT! ----------------- Capell lv070
All of his attacks can be parried, thus stunning him for a moment. Rucha was
enough to keep me healthy, and for extra insurance you can leave berry potions
and powders unlocked so that Balbagan and Komachi can use them as well.
-------------------- CONGRATULATIONS! YOU ARE AYATORIOUS! ---------------------

MAESTRO BATON is yours for defeating Vembert. At the bottom open two BSCH for
SCARIFICIAL DOLL, MEMOIRS OF A WARRIOR, then hop into the teleporter.

===============================================================================
SERAPHIC GATE, FLOOR #02 - ORADIAN DUNES
===============================================================================
ENEMIES                 | HP
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Dune Harpy              | 20000
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Fountain Beak           | 10000
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Quetzalcoatl            | 30000
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Fire Gigas              | 35000
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Face away from the warp pad and take a left around the rocks to greet some
enemies. Kill them, then take a right for a large clearing in the desert. In
the distance you'll see Fire Gigas and warp pad leading to Luce Plains (in
retrospect to real Oradian Dunes towards entrance of Zala).

Take a left (in retrospect heading towards Fayel) and press on towards the
place where Aya and Capell spent the night after leading Sapran refugees back
home. You'll encounter another Fire Gigas and another warp pad. Top Capell's HP
and MP, enchant some attack+ and HP regen bonuses, then step in warp pad.

===============================================================================
SERAPHIC GATE, FLOOR #03 - VESPLUME TOWER, TOP FLOOR
===============================================================================
ENEMIES                 | HP
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Shadow [spoiler]        | 130000
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Take a look at who you're facing!

------------------------ HERE COMES A NEW CHALLENGER! -------------------------
Main Combatant/s: SHADOW [SPOILER] [130000 HP]        EXP: 15000   FOL: 50000
        ELEM-RES: Air: 100, Fire: 100, Earth: 100, Aether: 100, Water: 100
          SKILLS: Skills names are spoilers.
Side Combatant/s: none
Environmental hazard: none
------------------------------ GET READY! FIGHT! ----------------- Capell lv073
Check that Grinn is set to B button, and then use it on the boss. As soon as
the hit lands, run away from him to possibly avoid boss' attack. If you get
hurt, no biggie as HP regen will top it back soon. Repeat as needed until he is
smoked.

Or you can let the boss come closer to you, wait for his attack to dodge it,
and the Grinn his ass to kingdom come.
-------------------- CONGRATULATIONS! YOU ARE AYATORIOUS! ---------------------

After showing him who's better, <BIG DADDY'S BACK> achievement is yours. Form
your party (don't include the newcomer yet, as his level is low, though he does
have some nice equipment). Reform with Rucha, Komachi and Balbagan.

There are two BSCH around with PIUS WOOD, GOLD BERRY POTION. Return to floor
#02 of SG.

===============================================================================
SERAPHIC GATE, FLOOR #02 - ORADIAN DUNES
===============================================================================

Kill Fire Gigas and its buddies in front of you, then head towards Fayel (in
retrospect). In the swirling sandstorm ahead is BSCH. Komachi Connect and
Honeysuckle it for AVIFIR HEADDRESS.

Return to Kolton, cos we're going to use newcomer's IC abilities with
Kristofer's for some nice acc. You'll need A Voucher in order to be able to buy
Amarlista. If not, skip this suggestion, but still return to Kolton to save
your game after coming this far to get final chr.

===============================================================================
KOLTON
===============================================================================

When you arrive, check out newcomer's gear: BALMUNG, CRYSTALLITE SUIT,
CRYSTALLITE HEADGEAR, CRYSTALLITE GREAVES.

Go to newcomer's IC and create 3x Lei and 3x Blossom Ring. Then Kristofer
Connect and go buy 3x Amarlista, then craft 3x Eternal Rose. It's babes-only
accessory with [HP regeneration 3%] and [MP regeneration 1%] abilities. Equip
it on all girls you're taking along and return to SG.

===============================================================================
SERAPHIC GATE, FLOOR #02 - ORADIAN DUNES
===============================================================================

In retrospect, head towards Zala until you bump into first Fire Gigas. Kill it,
then Balbagan Connect and Gigatackle cracked rock nearby for BSCH containing
ATLANTIS METAL. Check out nearby warp pad, but before going on, top your HP and
MP and enchant anti-fire or fire-absorb enchantments.

===============================================================================
SERAPHIC GATE, FLOOR #04 - LUCE PLAINS, N SIDE
===============================================================================
ENEMIES                 | HP
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Avalanche Harpy         | 30000
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Storm Gigas             | 40000
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Swordtail Viper         | 28000 (drops Dragon Fang)
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Gold Chest Mimic        | 50000
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Wyvern (BOSS)           | 500000
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Straight ahead is Wyvern, boss of the area. Immediately run towards its
location and engage in battle.

------------------------ HERE COMES A NEW CHALLENGER! -------------------------
Main Combatant/s: WYVERN [500000 HP]                  EXP: 26000   FOL: 20000
        ELEM-RES: Air: 100, Fire: -50, Earth: 100, Aether: 100, Water: 250
          SKILLS: Dragg Shot
                  Dragg Geyser
                  [Fireball]
                  [Tail swipe]
                  [Landing groundshake]
Side Combatant/s: regular enemies of this area
Environmental hazard: none
------------------------------ GET READY! FIGHT! ----------------- Capell lv080
Bring some equipment along that decreases fire damage (if you couldn't enchant
fire-proof or better), as fire is what Wyvern primarily relies upon. Stay away
from its head because it shoots very strong fireballs.

Wyvern starts the fight hovering just above ground. Wait until it lands, or
just start attacking it. When it lands, a shockwave is created around it for
some moderate damage. Stay to its side, and use Regins. Always be on the move
to avoid Dragg Geyser and Dragg Shot.

Once it becomes airborne again, wait for its next landing and let it have it.
-------------------- CONGRATULATIONS! YOU ARE AYATORIOUS! ---------------------

HROTTI is your reward for defeating Wyvern. There's out-of-reach BSCH on the
rocks ahead. Komachi Connect and Honeysuckle it for LUBRICUS CLOTH. Then check
on the other side of the hill to find BSCH with SARULEUS HELMET.

There is cracked rock in one side of the hill with MCH (turns into Gold Chest
Mimic), which can be abused for quick fol gathering.

In retrospect, head towards Graad Woods entrance.

Chad L. comments: First you'll need Balbagan in your group and the game has to
be beaten on normal or higher, because it requires the extra dungeon. Once
you've entered SG you'll want to get to the Luce Plains area, in that area
you'll find a cracked rock which contains a Gold Chest Mimic. This Mimic drops
between 57k to 61k. Now after defeating it go to the Mines section that can be
located in the next area after Luce Plains. In here you'll go up the steps and
defeat the crowd. At the top of the steps is a door to the right just before
the lift. Inside that door you'll find another Gold Chest Mimic. Once it is
defeated you'll reap between 57k and 61k again. Go back to Luce Plains and you
can repeat the process or just leave the mines and come back in and the Gold
Chest Mimic will reappear.

===============================================================================
SERAPHIC GATE, FLOOR #05 - BIHAR MINES
===============================================================================
ENEMIES                 | HP
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Lumper Count            | 15000
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Lumper King             | 25000
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Lumper Marquis          | 8000
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Lumper Duke             | 10000
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Lumper Baron            | 20000
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Gold Chest Mimic        | 50000
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

QUEST 48 CONTINUE - IC WRITING UPGRADE
This is the floor I want. You need 4x Placidus Wood from Lumper Dukes.
Immediately run forward and you'll spot a group of lumpers run upstairs. Go
after them, and while taking the stairs unsheathe your sword and Grinn them for
surprise. If not successful, no fret, just kill them all. Keep doing it until
you get 4+ Placidus Wood.

FOL TIP: Behind the door before taking first elevator is MCH (turns into Gold
Chest Mimic) which drops approximately 60000 fol when defeated. Exit is close,
so repeat as needed. Also enchant [Gold x3 / No EXP] enchantment to triple your
income.

Once you have the wood we need, exit SG and sail to Zala.

===============================================================================
ZALA
===============================================================================

QUEST 48 COMPLETION - IC WRITING UPGRADE
Michelle Connect and have her craft 2x Clerk's Quill (lv3 IC). Once you have
that, and assuming you still have Genius's Quills (one from Dais, one from
Plodhif Caverns), go see Rico and give him: 2x Clerk's Quill, Genius's Quill,
2x Lunatite, Amarlista... Your writing skills have improved!

Congratulations! You have now completely unlocked entire IC collection!

Now it's only the time needed to gather everything to craft everything for that
Compulsive achievement. Aya, hug me!

To be continued...

===============================================================================

09.)                         ACHIEVEMENTS - G0900
